<li id="cite_note-元太祖庙谥-112"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-元太祖庙谥_112-0"><sup><b>104.0</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-元太祖庙谥_112-1"><sup><b>104.1</b></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8B%E6%BF%82" title="宋濂">宋濂</a>. 《元史‧卷一‧本纪第一‧太祖》 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>至元三年冬十月，追谥圣武皇帝。至大二年冬十一月庚辰，加谥法天启运圣武皇帝，庙号太祖。在位二十二年。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E5%AE%8B%E6%BF%82&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E5%85%83%E5%8F%B2%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E4%B8%80%E2%80%A7%E6%9C%AC%E7%B4%80%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%80%E2%80%A7%E5%A4%AA%E7%A5%96%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-135"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-135">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8B%E6%BF%82" title="宋濂">宋濂</a>. 《元史‧卷三十七‧本纪第三十七‧宁宗》 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>宾天之日，皇后传顾命于太师、太平王、右丞相、答剌罕燕踮木儿，太保、浚宁王、知枢密院事伯颜等，谓圣体弥留，益推固让之初志，以宗社之重，属诸大兄忽都笃皇帝之世嫡。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E5%AE%8B%E6%BF%82&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E5%85%83%E5%8F%B2%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E4%B8%89%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E2%80%A7%E6%9C%AC%E7%B4%80%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E2%80%A7%E5%AF%A7%E5%AE%97%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-元惠宗庙号-137"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-元惠宗庙号_137-0"><sup><b>129.0</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-元惠宗庙号_137-1"><sup><b>129.1</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-元惠宗庙号_137-2"><sup><b>129.2</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-元惠宗庙号_137-3"><sup><b>129.3</b></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E5%8A%AD%E5%BF%9E" title="柯劭忞">柯劭忞</a>. 《新元史‧卷二十六‧本纪第二十六‧惠宗四昭宗》. <a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E8%8F%AF%E6%B0%91%E5%9C%8B" title="中华民国">中华民国</a> <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>丙戌，帝崩于应昌，在位三十七年，年五十有一。太尉完者、知枢密院事观音奴奉梓宫葬于起辇谷。群臣上庙号曰惠宗皇帝，国语曰乌哈图汗。明祖以帝能顺天命，退避而去，上尊谥曰顺帝。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E6%9F%AF%E5%8A%AD%E5%BF%9E&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E6%96%B0%E5%85%83%E5%8F%B2%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E2%80%A7%E6%9C%AC%E7%B4%80%E7%AC%AC%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E2%80%A7%E6%83%A0%E5%AE%97%E5%9B%9B%E6%98%AD%E5%AE%97%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.place=%E4%B8%AD%E8%8F%AF%E6%B0%91%E5%9C%8B&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>乌萨哈尔可汗，必力克图可汗的弟弟，名脱古思踮木儿。生于一三四二年（至正二年、壬午年）。于一三七九年（己未年） ，即可汗位，时年三十八岁。诏改明年为天元元年。于一三八八年（戊辰年）十月，被也速迭儿缢死。在位十年，享年四十七岁。谥号益宗，蒙古语称乌萨哈尔可汗。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E4%B8%AD%E5%9C%8B%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%8F%B2%E5%AD%B8%E6%9C%83&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E4%B8%AD%E5%9C%8B%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%8F%B2%E5%AD%B8%E6%9C%83%E8%AB%96%E6%96%87%E9%81%B8%E9%9B%86%EF%BC%881981%EF%BC%89%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.date=1986&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=%E7%AC%AC74%E9%A0%81&amp;rft.place=%E4%B8%AD%E8%8F%AF%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B&amp;rft.pub=%E5%85%A7%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E7%A4%BE&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com.tw%2Fbooks%3Fid%3D8yHTAAAAMAAJ%26q%3D%25E7%259B%258A%25E5%25AE%2597%25E8%2584%25AB%25E5%258F%25A4%25E6%2580%259D%26dq%3D%25E7%259B%258A%25E5%25AE%2597%25E8%2584%25AB%25E5%258F%25A4%25E6%2580%259D%26hl%3Dzh-TW%26sa%3DX%26ved%3D2ahUKEwiMv4jBsYPzAhUSBKYKHXnNCoE4FBDoAXoECAYQAg&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-蒙古世系谱-142"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-蒙古世系谱_142-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%9B%E6%98%B1" title="盛昱">盛昱</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20220222040217/https://books.google.com.tw/books?id=bi0qQgAACAAJ&amp;dq=%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E4%B8%96%E7%B3%BB%E8%AD%9C&amp;hl=zh-TW&amp;sa=X&amp;redir_esc=y" rel="nofollow">《蒙古世系谱‧卷四》</a>. （<a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.tw/books?id=bi0qQgAACAAJ&amp;dq=%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E4%B8%96%E7%B3%BB%E8%AD%9C&amp;hl=zh-TW&amp;sa=X&amp;redir_esc=y" rel="nofollow">原始内容</a>存档于2022-02-22） <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>必里克图汗者，哲宗也。按谱，惠宗殂，哲宗继立，是即爱育识里达腊，改元宣光，洪武十一年六月殂。传位脱古斯踮木儿，改元天元，谱中之乌萨哈尔汗也。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E7%9B%9B%E6%98%B1&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E4%B8%96%E7%B3%BB%E8%AD%9C%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E5%9B%9B%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com.tw%2Fbooks%3Fid%3Dbi0qQgAACAAJ%26dq%3D%25E8%2592%2599%25E5%258F%25A4%25E4%25B8%2596%25E7%25B3%25BB%25E8%25AD%259C%26hl%3Dzh-TW%26sa%3DX%26redir_esc%3Dy&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-148"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-148">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B6%99%E9%9B%B2%E7%94%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="赵云田（页面不存在）">赵云田</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20211214091907/https://books.google.com.tw/books?id=_YR0AAAAIAAJ&amp;q=%E5%B2%B1%E7%B8%BD%E6%B1%97+%E8%84%AB%E8%84%AB%E4%B8%8D%E8%8A%B1&amp;dq=%E5%B2%B1%E7%B8%BD%E6%B1%97+%E8%84%AB%E8%84%AB%E4%B8%8D%E8%8A%B1&amp;hl=zh-TW&amp;sa=X&amp;ved=2ahUKEwjD26WvvI_zAhVGxYsBHQiACTQQ6AF6BAgDEAI" rel="nofollow">《北疆通史‧第二卷》</a>. 中华人民共和国: <a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E5%B7%9E%E5%8F%A4%E7%B1%8D%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E7%A4%BE" title="中州古籍出版社">中州古籍出版社</a>. : 第387页. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/9787534818929" title="Special:网络书源/9787534818929"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 9787534818929</a>. （<a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.tw/books?id=_YR0AAAAIAAJ&amp;q=%E5%B2%B1%E7%B8%BD%E6%B1%97+%E8%84%AB%E8%84%AB%E4%B8%8D%E8%8A%B1&amp;dq=%E5%B2%B1%E7%B8%BD%E6%B1%97+%E8%84%AB%E8%84%AB%E4%B8%8D%E8%8A%B1&amp;hl=zh-TW&amp;sa=X&amp;ved=2ahUKEwjD26WvvI_zAhVGxYsBHQiACTQQ6AF6BAgDEAI" rel="nofollow">原始内容</a>存档于2021-12-14） <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>最高君主为可汗，当时脱欢、也先立元裔脱脱不花为可汗，称「岱总汗」（一说为太宗汗的音译）。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E8%B6%99%E9%9B%B2%E7%94%B0&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E5%8C%97%E7%96%86%E9%80%9A%E5%8F%B2%E2%80%A7%E7%AC%AC%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%B7%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=9787534818929&amp;rft.pages=%E7%AC%AC387%E9%A0%81&amp;rft.place=%E4%B8%AD%E8%8F%AF%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9C%8B&amp;rft.pub=%E4%B8%AD%E5%B7%9E%E5%8F%A4%E7%B1%8D%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E7%A4%BE&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com.tw%2Fbooks%3Fid%3D_YR0AAAAIAAJ%26q%3D%25E5%25B2%25B1%25E7%25B8%25BD%25E6%25B1%2597%2B%25E8%2584%25AB%25E8%2584%25AB%25E4%25B8%258D%25E8%258A%25B1%26dq%3D%25E5%25B2%25B1%25E7%25B8%25BD%25E6%25B1%2597%2B%25E8%2584%25AB%25E8%2584%25AB%25E4%25B8%258D%25E8%258A%25B1%26hl%3Dzh-TW%26sa%3DX%26ved%3D2ahUKEwjD26WvvI_zAhVGxYsBHQiACTQQ6AF6BAgDEAI&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-149"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-149">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BC%B5%E5%BB%B7%E7%8E%89" title="张廷玉">张廷玉</a>. 《明史‧卷三百二十八‧列传第二百十六‧外国九 瓦剌‧朵颜福余 泰宁》 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>明年冬，也先自立为可汗，以其次子为太师，来朝，书称大元田盛大可汗，末曰添元元年。田盛，犹言天圣也。报书称曰瓦剌可汗。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E5%BC%B5%E5%BB%B7%E7%8E%89&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E6%98%8E%E5%8F%B2%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E4%B8%89%E7%99%BE%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AB%E2%80%A7%E5%88%97%E5%82%B3%E7%AC%AC%E4%BA%8C%E7%99%BE%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E2%80%A7%E5%A4%96%E5%9C%8B%E4%B9%9D+%E7%93%A6%E5%89%8C%E2%80%A7%E6%9C%B5%E9%A1%8F%E7%A6%8F%E4%BD%99+%E6%B3%B0%E5%AF%A7%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-150"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-150">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%90%A8%E5%86%88" title="萨冈">萨冈</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/06054742.cn/page/n42/mode/2up?view=theater" rel="nofollow">《钦定蒙古源流‧卷五》</a>. : 第43页 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>岱总汗续娶之福晋萨睦尔太后生一子，名蒙古勒克哷青吉斯，丙寅年生，年七嵗贮于皮柜，以马负之，伊母萨睦尔福晋持刀带领骑牛、乘马及步兵出师，由库奎扎巴哈往伐四卫喇特，大有俘获，撤兵而回，即奉蒙古勒克哷青吉斯台吉即位，维时七嵗，称为乌珂克图汗。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E8%96%A9%E5%B2%A1&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E6%AC%BD%E5%AE%9A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E6%BA%90%E6%B5%81%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E4%BA%94%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=%E7%AC%AC43%E9%A0%81&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Farchive.org%2Fdetails%2F06054742.cn%2Fpage%2Fn42%2Fmode%2F2up%3Fview%3Dtheater&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-151"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-151">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%90%A8%E5%86%88" title="萨冈">萨冈</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/06054742.cn/page/n46/mode/2up?view=theater" rel="nofollow">《钦定蒙古源流‧卷五》</a>. : 第46页 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>摩伦汗，自癸酉至甲戌，在位二载年，十八嵗殁。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E8%96%A9%E5%B2%A1&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E6%AC%BD%E5%AE%9A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E6%BA%90%E6%B5%81%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E4%BA%94%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=%E7%AC%AC46%E9%A0%81&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Farchive.org%2Fdetails%2F06054742.cn%2Fpage%2Fn46%2Fmode%2F2up%3Fview%3Dtheater&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-152"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-152">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BC%B5%E5%BB%B7%E7%8E%89" title="张廷玉">张廷玉</a>. 《明史‧卷三百二十八‧列传第二百十六‧外国八 鞑靼》 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>亦思马因死，入寇者复称小王子，又有伯颜猛可王。弘治元年夏，小王子奉书求贡，自称大元大可汗。朝廷方务优容，许之。自是，与伯颜猛可王等屡入贡，渐往来套中，出没为寇。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E5%BC%B5%E5%BB%B7%E7%8E%89&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E6%98%8E%E5%8F%B2%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E4%B8%89%E7%99%BE%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AB%E2%80%A7%E5%88%97%E5%82%B3%E7%AC%AC%E4%BA%8C%E7%99%BE%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E2%80%A7%E5%A4%96%E5%9C%8B%E5%85%AB+%E9%9F%83%E9%9D%BC%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-153"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-153">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%90%A8%E5%86%88" title="萨冈">萨冈</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/06054742.cn/page/n55/mode/2up?view=theater" rel="nofollow">《钦定蒙古源流‧卷五》</a>. : 第55页–第56页 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>满都海彻辰福晋，系戊午年生，年三十三嵗，巴图䝉克，系甲申年生，年七嵗，定为夫妇。本年庚寅，因欲占据达延国，遂称为达延汗，于老福晋前即汗位。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E8%96%A9%E5%B2%A1&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E6%AC%BD%E5%AE%9A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E6%BA%90%E6%B5%81%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E4%BA%94%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=%E7%AC%AC55%E9%A0%81-%E7%AC%AC56%E9%A0%81&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Farchive.org%2Fdetails%2F06054742.cn%2Fpage%2Fn55%2Fmode%2F2up%3Fview%3Dtheater&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-154"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-154">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a href="/wiki/%E9%84%AD%E5%A4%A9%E6%8C%BA" title="郑天挺">郑天挺</a>; <li id="cite_note-155"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-155">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%90%A8%E5%86%88" title="萨冈">萨冈</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/06054742.cn/page/n75/mode/1up?view=theater" rel="nofollow">《钦定蒙古源流‧卷六》</a>. : 第75页–第76页 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>子博迪台吉，生于甲子年，至甲辰年，四十一岁即位，科尔沁之巴图尔摩罗齐建议右翼，原系强斡之俦或征掠，以离散之或酌量入于左翼，均分之博迪阿拉克汗。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E8%96%A9%E5%B2%A1&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E6%AC%BD%E5%AE%9A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E6%BA%90%E6%B5%81%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E5%85%AD%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=%E7%AC%AC75%E9%A0%81-%E7%AC%AC76%E9%A0%81&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Farchive.org%2Fdetails%2F06054742.cn%2Fpage%2Fn75%2Fmode%2F1up%3Fview%3Dtheater&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-156"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-156">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%90%A8%E5%86%88" title="萨冈">萨冈</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/06054742.cn/page/n78/mode/1up?view=theater" rel="nofollow">《钦定蒙古源流‧卷六》</a>. : 第79页 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>长子达赉逊库登台吉，甲辰年生，岁次壬申年，二十九岁，于白室前称汗号，与右翼三万人和睦相㑹。而旋，阿拉克第二子阿勒坦来迎向汗求赐号，云今统治已平，原有䕶卫汗治索多汗小汗之号，祈即将此号赐我，我情愿䕶卫大统，汗然之，遂与以索多汗之号，由是库登汗之号……</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E8%96%A9%E5%B2%A1&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E6%AC%BD%E5%AE%9A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E6%BA%90%E6%B5%81%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E5%85%AD%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=%E7%AC%AC79%E9%A0%81&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Farchive.org%2Fdetails%2F06054742.cn%2Fpage%2Fn78%2Fmode%2F1up%3Fview%3Dtheater&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-157"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-157">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%90%A8%E5%86%88" title="萨冈">萨冈</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/06054742.cn/page/n79/mode/1up?view=theater" rel="nofollow">《钦定蒙古源流‧卷六》</a>. : 第80页–第81页 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>图们台吉，乙亥年生，岁次癸夘年，二十九岁即位，岁次壬子年，三十八岁，往见盘结腰刀之噶尔玛喇嘛，遂受禅教聚集六万人，传示大政，令左翼三万人内，察哈尔之阿穆岱鸿台吉、喀尔喀之卫征索博该；右翼三万人内，鄂尔多斯之库图克台彻辰鸿台吉、阿苏特之诺木达喇古拉齐诺延、土默特之楚噜克鸿台吉执政理事，遂称为扎萨克图汗。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E8%96%A9%E5%B2%A1&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E6%AC%BD%E5%AE%9A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E6%BA%90%E6%B5%81%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E5%85%AD%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=%E7%AC%AC80%E9%A0%81-%E7%AC%AC81%E9%A0%81&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Farchive.org%2Fdetails%2F06054742.cn%2Fpage%2Fn79%2Fmode%2F1up%3Fview%3Dtheater&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-158"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-158">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%90%A8%E5%86%88" title="萨冈">萨冈</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/06054742.cn/page/n80/mode/1up?view=theater" rel="nofollow">《钦定蒙古源流‧卷六》</a>. : 第81页 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>布延台吉，己夘年生，岁次丁巳年，三十九岁即位，大众称为彻辰汗。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E8%96%A9%E5%B2%A1&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E6%AC%BD%E5%AE%9A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E6%BA%90%E6%B5%81%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E5%85%AD%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=%E7%AC%AC81%E9%A0%81&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Farchive.org%2Fdetails%2F06054742.cn%2Fpage%2Fn80%2Fmode%2F1up%3Fview%3Dtheater&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-159"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-159">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%90%A8%E5%86%88" title="萨冈">萨冈</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/06054742.cn/page/n81/mode/1up?view=theater" rel="nofollow">《钦定蒙古源流‧卷六》</a>. : 第82页 <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到中文网页">（中文）</span>. <q>长子陵丹巴图尔台吉，壬辰年生，岁次甲辰年，十三岁即位，大众称为库图克图汗。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;rft.au=%E8%96%A9%E5%B2%A1&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E6%AC%BD%E5%AE%9A%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E6%BA%90%E6%B5%81%E2%80%A7%E5%8D%B7%E5%85%AD%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=%E7%AC%AC82%E9%A0%81&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Farchive.org%2Fdetails%2F06054742.cn%2Fpage%2Fn81%2Fmode%2F1up%3Fview%3Dtheater&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<h3><span id=".E6.9D.A5.E6.BA.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="来源">来源</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="编辑章节：来源">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r61209943">.mw-parser-output .refbegin{font-size:90%;margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-hanging-indents>ul{list-style-type:none;margin-left:0}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-hanging-indents>ul>li,.mw-parser-output .refbegin-hanging-indents>dl>dd{margin-left:0;padding-left:3.2em;text-indent:-3.2em;list-style:none}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-100{font-size:100%}</style><div class="refbegin" style="">
<dl><dt>书籍</dt></dl>
<ul><li>［法国］<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8B%92%E5%86%85%C2%B7%E6%A0%BC%E9%B2%81%E5%A1%9E" title="勒内·格鲁塞">勒内·格鲁塞</a> 着，蓝琪 译：《<a href="/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E5%8E%9F%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD" title="草原帝国">草原帝国</a>》，1995年出版.</li>
<li>［法国］勒内·格鲁塞 着，龚钺 译：《<a href="/wiki/%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD%E5%8F%B2" title="蒙古帝国史">蒙古帝国史</a>》，1986年出版.</li>
<li>［伊朗］<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BF%97%E8%B4%B9%E5%B0%BC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="志费尼（页面不存在）">志费尼</a> 着，何高济 译：《<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%96%E7%95%8C%E5%BE%81%E6%9C%8D%E8%80%85%E5%8F%B2" title="世界征服者史">世界征服者史</a>》，<a href="/wiki/%E5%95%86%E5%8A%A1%E5%8D%B0%E4%B9%A6%E9%A6%86" title="商务印书馆">商务印书馆</a>2004年出版.</li></ul>
</div>

</td>
<td align="center" width="40%"><b> 大蒙古国<br/><small>1206年春－1368年8月<br/><a href="/wiki/%E5%85%83%E6%9C%9D" title="元朝">大元</a>（1271年－1368年）<br/><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9B%9B%E5%A4%A7%E6%B1%97%E5%9B%BD" title="四大汗国">四大汗国</a>（13世纪－14世纪）</small></b>

<p><span class="nowrap"> <a href="/wiki/%E6%88%90%E5%90%89%E6%80%9D%E6%B1%97" title="成吉思汗">成吉思汗</a>（<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BC%E5%80%AB" title="尼伦">黄金家族</a>） </span> <span class="nowrap">→  <a class="mw-selflink selflink">蒙古帝国</a>（<a href="/wiki/%E8%92%99%E5%8F%A4%E5%BE%81%E6%88%B0" title="蒙古征战">扩张</a><span style="white-space:nowrap; font-weight:bold;"> ·</span> <a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E5%B1%A0%E6%9D%80%E5%88%97%E8%A1%A8" title="大屠杀列表">屠杀</a>）</span> <span class="nowrap">→ <a href="/wiki/%E5%85%83%E6%9C%9D" title="元朝">元朝</a>（<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8B%E5%85%83%E6%88%98%E4%BA%89" title="宋元战争">灭宋</a><span style="white-space:nowrap; font-weight:bold;"> ·</span> <a href="/wiki/%E5%85%83%E6%97%A5%E6%88%98%E4%BA%89" title="元日战争">侵日</a>） </span> <span class="nowrap">→  <a href="/wiki/%E5%8C%97%E5%85%83" title="北元">北元</a>
